1. use chatgpt to create simple version of picture of tokens
1b. Or get the picture from 
    - https://dice-throne.rulepop.com/#tokens
    - Upload code to https://jsfiddle.net/
2. use gimp to edit out unneeded parts
3. convert png to svt

https://www.pngtosvg.com/
https://www.adobe.com/express/feature/image/convert/png-to-svg



specs
icon height on token 0.4mm

blank token 22 x 22 x 2.3

Steps:
1. right click and merge
2. go into assembly mode
3. click "center coincidence"
4. parallel_distance = 0.4
